We will show our work at each step.

When evaluating an expression, you must first evaluate the expressions inside parentheses, then exponents, then multiplication and division from left to right, and finally addition and subtraction from left to right. For example, to evaluate the expression 3 + 4 × 2, you would first multiply 4 × 2 to get 8, and then add 3 to get 11.
